56b6(1): pa yin zhe na/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' ye shes yongs su dag pa dang / zhing rnyog pa med pas sems can gyi khams la rnam par lta ste/ des de na sems ca

58b5(1): las 'das pa'i ye shes phun sum tshogs pa yin no// rigs kyi bu chos bcu po de dag dang ldan na/ byang chub sems dpa' ye shes phun sum tshogs pa rnams yin no//

58b7(1): sems can thams kyi 'tsho bar gyur pa rnams yin/ gnod pa dang lan du phan 'dogs pa dang bral ba rnams yin/ chos kyi sprin chen po kun zad pa rnams yin/ sems
58b8(1): thams cad kyi gnas su gyur pa rnams yin/ de ba'i chos rnams kyi sa bon gyi gzhir gyur pa rnams yani/ rin po che'i snod du gyur pa rnams yin/ rtsi chen po'i snod
58'a1(1): du gyur pa rnams yin/ mi bskul ba rnams yin/ mi sdang ba rnams yin no// rigs kyi bu de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' yangs shing tshad med pa

59a3(1): bon gyi gzhir gyur pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' rin po che'i sdod du gyur pa yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lte ste dper na sa chen po ni rin po che rnam pa
59a4(1): sna tshogs kyi sdong yin te/ sa chen po la rin po che sna tshogs kun snang ngo // de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang yon tan rin pa ci rnam pa sna tshogs kyi sdong du gyur
59a5(1): pa yin te/ byang chub sems dpa' la yon tan rin po che sna tshogs kun snang ste/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' rin po che'i snod du gyur pa yin no// ji ltar na/

59a7(1): sa chen po la gnas te 'jig rten na snang ngo // de bzhin du gang dag gis nyon mongs pa'i nang rnam pa sna tshogs pa rnams ni bar 'gyur ba'i chos kyi kyi chen po rnams kya
